### [39] [From Tokens to States: LLMs as a Special Case of World Models and the Continuous Path Beyond](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28127)
*Paul Dubois*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出LLM与世界模型并非互斥关系，而是构成了一个连续频谱。LLM只是其中的特例，研究指出应通过缓解LLM的约束向更广义的世界模型演进，并分析了此过程中在数据规模和架构适配性方面面临的重大挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在挑战当前AI社区将大语言模型（LLM）与世界模型视为对立范式的观点，纠正“LLM预测token，世界模型模拟现实”这种非黑即白的二分法，为通往通用人工智能（AGI）的架构演进提供理论框架。

Method: 本文采用理论分析法，首先通过定义LLM作为世界模型的退化特例来解构二元对立论点；其次，通过构建从下一token预测（NTP）到联合嵌入预测架构（JEPA）的连续频谱，论证了两者之间存在多种中间形态；最后，针对扩展此频谱所面临的“数据悬崖”和“架构普适性”问题进行了深入探讨。

Result: 1. 证明了LLM是世界模型的特殊形式，即状态空间为所有token序列，动作仅为添加一个token；2. 识别出一条从NTP到JEPA的演进路径，涵盖了多token预测、未来摘要预测等多种中间研究方向；3. 明确了向更通用世界模型演进过程中的核心障碍：从文本数据转向行动标记环境的数据获取难题，以及Transformer架构在连续状态空间预测中的局限性。

Conclusion: LLM与世界模型并非二元对立，而是存在一个连续的频谱。LLM是世界模型的一种退化特例，未来研究应聚焦于如何在大规模自监督学习与向连续状态空间预测演进之间取得平衡，解决数据获取与架构适配的挑战。

Abstract: The AI community has framed the relationship between large language models (LLMs) and world models as a dichotomy: LLMs predict tokens; world models simulate reality. Yann LeCun argues in 2022 that reaching general intelligence requires abandoning autoregressive token prediction in favour of latent-space architectures. This framing is unnecessarily binary. Two claims will be defended. First, LLMs are a degenerate special case of world models: the state space is the set of all token sequences, the only action is appending one token, and world models are therefore a strict generalisation of LLMs, not a replacement. Second, there is a natural continuous spectrum from NTP to JEPA, with multi-token prediction, future-summary prediction, and next-latent prediction as intermediate stations already populated by current research. Moving along this spectrum relaxes the LLM constraints one by one. It also progressively surrenders the two practical advantages that make LLMs trainable at scale: internet-scale self-supervised data, and a transformer architecture co-designed for discrete token prediction. Both are examined as open research questions: the data question (the cliff from self-supervised text to instrumented action-labelled environments) and the architecture question (whether the transformer generalises to continuous-state prediction, or whether a new primitive is needed).

</details>


### [40] [Cognitive Episodes in LLM Reasoning Traces Enable Interpretable Human Item Difficulty Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28186)
*Chenguang Wang,Ming Li,Xinyue Zeng,Zhuochun Li,Hong Jiao,Tianyi Zhou,Dawei Zhou*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Epi2Diff是一种通过分析大推理模型的认知轨迹片段来预测题目难度的框架，它超越了传统的文本表示方法，在准确性和可解释性上取得了显著优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有题目难度预测方法多依赖昂贵的人工校准或单一的文本表示，缺乏对题目诱发的认知负担和解题过程的深入分析。研究者旨在通过利用LRM提供的推理轨迹，揭示影响题目难度的潜在认知过程。

Method: 提出了Epi2Diff（Episode to Difficulty）框架，将LRM的推理轨迹映射为具有认知意义的片段序列。该方法通过分析推理规模、努力分配和状态转换，提取紧凑的片段动态特征，并将其与题目语义表示相结合，用于预测人类题目难度。

Result: 在四个真实世界题目难度数据集上的实验表明，Epi2Diff的表现始终优于微调的小模型、LLM上下文学习和监督式LLM微调基线；在SAT派生的分类基准上，相对提升了8.1%。分析显示，难题往往对应更具努力性、迭代性和侧重执行的片段动态，而非仅仅是更长的回答。

Conclusion: Epi2Diff证明了利用大推理模型（LRM）生成的推理轨迹，并将其转化为认知导向的片段序列，能够显著提升人类题目难度预测的准确性与可解释性。这一框架为教育测评领域提供了一种全新的基于认知过程的测量视角。

Abstract: Predicting human item difficulty is central to educational assessment, where reliable estimates support fairness and effective test construction. Existing methods often depend on costly human calibration or item-level textual representations, providing limited evidence about the cognitive processes that make items difficult. We argue that difficulty should be viewed not only as a property of item text, but also as an observable consequence of the problem-solving burden an item induces. Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) offer scalable process evidence through reasoning traces, but such evidence must be structured to support interpretable modeling. To this end, we introduce Epi2Diff (Episode to Difficulty), a framework that maps LRM reasoning traces into cognitively grounded episode sequences. These episodes group trace segments into functional problem-solving states, enabling difficulty to be modeled through reasoning scale, effort allocation, and state transitions. Epi2Diff extracts compact episode-dynamic features and combines them with semantic item representations for human difficulty prediction. Experiments on four real-world human difficulty datasets show that Epi2Diff consistently outperforms strong baselines, including fine-tuned small language models, LLM in-context learning, and supervised LLM adaptation. On SAT-derived classification benchmarks, Epi2Diff achieves an 8.1% average relative gain over supervised LLM fine-tuning baselines. Further analyses show that harder items induce more effortful, iterative, and implementation-centered episode dynamics, rather than merely longer responses. These results demonstrate that cognitive episodes in LRM reasoning traces provide a predictive and interpretable process representation for human item difficulty, offering a new lens for educational measurement with reasoning models.

</details>


### [41] [Vision-Default, Prior-Override: Causal Mechanisms of Perception-Knowledge Conflict in Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28273)
*Niclas Lietzow,Danielle Bitterman,Carsten Eickhoff,William Rudman,Michal Golovanevsky*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究通过细粒度机理分析揭示了 VLM 处理感知与知识冲突的内在逻辑：模型默认倾向于视觉接地，而利用极少数特定的注意力头来实现基于世界知识的推断，这种非对称结构在不同模型规模和家族中表现高度一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多模态大模型在视觉证据与记忆中的世界知识发生冲突时，缺乏对其内部运作机制的因果性解释。为了提升多模态系统的可靠性，必须理解模型是如何在组件层面化解这种感知与知识冲突的。

Method: 研究采用了结合激活修补（activation patching）、模型组件消融（ablation）以及机理分析（mechanistic analysis）的方法。具体涵盖了残差流、注意力头以及 MLP 子层三个层级的细粒度分析，通过在三个主流 VLM 模型家族上的实验，追踪了模型在面对感知与知识冲突时的信息流向，并定位了关键的因果组件。

Result: 研究发现：1. 视觉接地是默认行为；2. 知识引导依赖于极少数（2.5%-4.8%）特定的注意力头，这些头主要集中在网络后半部分；3. 通过消融这些关键头，在知识引导提示下，68%-96% 的预测会转变为视觉引导，而视觉引导的预测仅受 0.8%-7.5% 的影响，表现出高度的非对称性；4. 这些注意力头可进一步分解为负责调节信息流的“路由头”和负责投影答案的“写入头”。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了多模态大模型（VLM）在处理感知与知识冲突时存在一个稀疏的因果回路。视觉接地是模型的默认行为，而知识引导则依赖于网络后半部分中极少数特定的注意力头。这种非对称的因果结构表明，VLM 的知识注入是模块化且可定位的，为提高多模态模型的鲁棒性和可解释性提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Vision-language models must reconcile visual evidence with memorized world knowledge when the two conflict. How they resolve this conflict shapes the reliability of multimodal systems, yet prior work characterizes it behaviorally without a component-level causal account. We combine activation patching across three granularities (residual stream, attention heads, and MLP sublayers) with model-component ablation studies and mechanistic analysis. Across three VLM families, we find that visual grounding emerges by default, whereas prior grounding depends on a small set of causally necessary attention heads (2.5-4.8%) concentrated in the second half of the network. These heads enable answers from stored world knowledge (e.g., "red" for a strawberry) despite conflicting visual input. Ablating them flips predictions from knowledge-grounded to visually grounded answers in 68-96% of cases under prior-knowledge prompts, but changes only 0.8-7.5% of visually grounded predictions, establishing an asymmetric causal structure. The identified heads decompose into routing heads, which modulate information flow, and writing heads, which directly project answer tokens into the residual stream. This structure is consistent across model families and scales, revealing a sparse causal circuit underlying perception-knowledge conflict in VLMs.

</details>

### [42] [A Sensitivity-Aware Test Collection for Search Among Personal Information](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27559)
*Jack McKechnie,Graham McDonald,Craig Macdonald*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者通过众包方式为Enron邮件语料库标注了150个查询及11,471个相关性判断；利用大语言模型（LLM）进一步扩展了数据集的规模，涵盖了相关性评估和敏感性标签；并提供了基于该数据集的基准性能测试及预构建的稀疏和稠密检索索引。

Result: 构建了包含150个查询、50个主题及约1.1万余条人工标注的相关性评估数据集；成功整合入ir_datasets工具包；在Huggingface上发布了预构建的索引，并提供了基准实验结果供后续研究参考。

Conclusion: 该论文成功构建了一个包含查询、相关性标注及敏感性标签的Enron数据集，为敏感信息感知检索（SAS）任务提供了一个标准化的评估基准，并开源了相关资源以促进该领域的研究。

Abstract: Traditional search tasks aim to satisfy user information needs by returning a subset of a collection of documents, ranked by the documents' relevance to a user query. However, some collections that contain useful information also contain sensitive personal information. Recently, there has been increasing interest in the development of Sensitivity-Aware Search (SAS) retrieval models to provide users with effective retrieval results without revealing such sensitive information. To develop such systems, test collections containing both sensitive and non-sensitive information, a set of queries, and query-document relevance assessments are required. The Enron email corpus contains real business-related emails, where some emails also contain sensitive personal information. However, the original Enron collection does not contain queries or query-relevance assessments. To this end, we crowdsource 150 query formulations for 50 different topics and 11,471 query-relevance assessments for a subset of the Enron documents that have been manually labelled for sensitivity. We follow best practices for using large language models (LLMs) in Information Retrieval evaluation to extend the collection further with additional LLM judged query-relevance assessments and sensitivity labels. We present baseline performances for relevance, sensitivity classification, and sensitivity-aware search on the collection. We make the collection available, including through the popular ir_datasets package, and provide pre-built sparse and dense indices on Huggingface to facilitate easy experimentation.

### [43] [Intuition-Guided Latent Reasoning for LLM-Based Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27684)
*Chang Liu,Yimeng Bai,Xiaoyan Zhao,Yang Zhang,Qifan Wang,Fuli Feng,Wenge Rong*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对大模型在推荐系统潜空间推理中起点缺乏约束的问题，本文提出了IntuRec框架，通过将Top-K推荐候选集转化为“直觉嵌入”来锚定推理起点，有效提升了推荐的准确性和推理效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于潜空间推理的推荐方法存在严重的对齐问题，即推理过程的初始点往往是无约束的，导致推理轨迹偏离目标物品的真实嵌入空间，从而限制了模型的推荐性能。作者希望通过借鉴认知神经科学中“直觉作为潜在先验”的理念来解决这一问题。

Method: 提出了一种名为IntuRec的两阶段框架：
1. 提取阶段：利用LLM根据用户历史生成Top-K候选集，作为“推荐直觉”的来源。
2. 注入阶段：通过自注意力和交叉注意力机制，将候选集转换为与偏好对齐的“直觉嵌入”（Intuition Embedding），以此作为潜空间推理的锚定起点，引导后续推理路径。

Result: 实验结果表明，IntuRec在多个真实世界数据集上的表现显著优于当前主流的推荐系统基线模型，验证了该框架在引导大语言模型进行精准潜空间推理方面的有效性。

Conclusion: IntuRec通过引入“推荐直觉”机制，成功解决了LLM在潜空间推理中初始点无约束、与目标物品表示对齐困难的问题，证明了认知科学启发下的先验知识能有效增强大语言模型在推荐系统中的推理性能。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated impressive reasoning capabilities in complex problem-solving tasks, motivating their use for preference reasoning in recommender systems. Latent reasoning, which operates in continuous hidden spaces rather than discrete tokens, has recently emerged as a promising paradigm for LLM-based recommendation. However, existing methods often start from unconstrained reasoning points, where hidden representations are misaligned with target item embeddings, leading to suboptimal reasoning trajectories.
  Inspired by cognitive neuroscience, which suggests that human multi-step reasoning is guided by intuition as a latent prior, we propose \emph{IntuRec}, a two-stage framework that anchors latent reasoning with \emph{recommendation intuition}. In the extraction stage, the LLM-based recommender generates a top-$K$ candidate set based on users' histories as the source of intuition. In the injection stage, the candidate set is transformed into a preference-aligned intuition embedding using self- and cross-attention mechanisms, which initializes the reasoning start point and guides subsequent latent reasoning. By providing a semantically grounded starting point, IntuRec efficiently explores the preference space along more accurate reasoning trajectories. Extensive experiments on multiple real-world datasets demonstrate that IntuRec consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines. We release our code at https://github.com/Ten-Mao/IntuRec.

</details>


### [44] [Bifocal Diffusion Language Models: Asymmetric Bidirectional Context for Parallel Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27732)
*Yuhang Chen,Xianfeng Wu,Jinhao Duan,Mingfu Liang,Xiaohan Wei,Yunchen Pu,Fei Tian,Chonglin Sun,Parish Aggarwal,Frank Shyu,Luke Simon,Sandeep Pandey,Xi Liu,Tianlong Chen*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出R2LM（从右向左Mamba）架构，通过非对称双向上下文设计，在支持KV缓存实现高效并行推理的同时，引入反向SSM获取右侧上下文以保障生成质量，完美解决了离散扩散语言模型在推理效率与生成质量间的权衡难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 离散扩散语言模型（dLLMs）虽能实现并行生成以提升速度，但面临架构设计困境：双向注意力虽生成质量高但不支持KV缓存，严重限制了推理吞吐量；因果注意力虽支持KV缓存但丢失了右侧上下文信息，导致生成质量下降。研究旨在打破这一性能与效率的平衡壁垒。

Method: 提出了一种名为“双焦点”（Bifocal）的架构范式，并具体实现为“从右向左Mamba”（R2LM）。该方法采用非对称双向上下文设计：一方面使用标准因果注意力（Causal Attention）获取精确的左侧上下文并支持KV缓存，另一方面利用轻量级的反向Mamba状态空间模型（SSM）作为辅助分支，提供压缩后的右侧上下文，从而在不破坏缓存能力的前提下引入了未来信息。

Result: 在Qwen3-1.7B模型及60B token的实验中，R2LM表现优异：在批量推理场景下，其吞吐量比双向dLLMs高出2.4倍至12.9倍，比自回归（AR）基线快1.9倍至2.9倍；在生成质量上，不仅全面超越因果基线，平均表现还优于双向dLLM。

Conclusion: R2LM成功解决了离散扩散语言模型在生成质量与推理效率之间的矛盾。通过引入非对称双向上下文机制，R2LM在保持高性能的同时，实现了与KV缓存的兼容性，为高效的并行生成提供了一种全新的、极具竞争力的架构范式。

Abstract: Discrete diffusion language models (dLLMs) recover masked tokens in parallel, offering significant speedups over autoregressive (AR) generation. However, such promising frameworks face a fundamental architectural design dilemma: \ding{182} Adopting bidirectional attention achieves strong generation quality by allowing each position to access the full context, but is inherently incompatible with KV caching, limiting inference throughput in batch-serving scenarios; \ding{183} Conversely, causal attention enables efficient cached inference but loses all right-side context, substantially degrading generation quality. This paper introduces Bifocal dLLMs, a new paradigm that resolves this dilemma through \emph{asymmetric bidirectional context}. Analogous to bifocal lenses, we instantiate the paradigm as \textbf{R2LM} (Right-to-Left Mamba), which combines two complementary mechanisms: $a$) standard causal attention providing precise left-context with full KV cache compatibility, while $b$) a lightweight reverse Mamba SSM sidecar supplying compressed right-side context without breaking cacheability. Comprehensive experiments on continued pretraining of Qwen3-1.7B with 60B tokens demonstrate that R2LM achieves $2.4\times$ to $12.9\times$ higher throughput than bidirectional dLLMs and $1.9\times$ to $2.9\times$ speedup over AR baselines in batch serving through parallel decoding with KV caching, while exceeding the causal baseline on most benchmarks and surpassing the bidirectional dLLM on average.

</details>


### [45] [End-to-End Dynamic Sparsity for Resource-Adaptive LLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27743)
*Yuhang Chen,Jinhao Duan,Ruichen Zhang,Mingfu Liang,Xiaohan Wei,Yunchen Pu,Fei Tian,Chonglin Sun,Parish Aggarwal,Frank Shyu,Luke Simon,Sandeep Pandey,Tianlong Chen,Xi Liu*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对云端计算资源的动态波动，本文提出了 L2A 框架，通过引入输入感知与预算感知的门控机制，实现大模型推理过程中对深度、吞吐量和延迟的动态自适应调整，在保证任务准确性的前提下显著提升了资源利用效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型推理通常基于静态资源假设，无法应对云端环境中的资源波动（如竞价实例抢占）或不同的服务质量要求。静态模型在资源紧张时易崩溃，而在资源充足时又造成计算浪费，缺乏灵活性。

Method: 提出了 L2A（Learning to Allocate）端到端框架，通过集成轻量级的、条件化的门控网络，将模型推理转化为基于输入内容与实时资源预算的受限分配问题。该方法同时优化层跳过（内存/深度控制）、注意力头剪枝（吞吐量控制）和推理标记减少（延迟控制）三个维度，并通过联合目标函数进行训练。

Result: 在 Llama-3-8B 和 Qwen-3-4B 模型上，L2A 能够覆盖完整的计算-精度帕累托边界。在实现高达 34% 的层稀疏度时，GSM8K 基准测试的性能与稠密模型差距仅为 0.6% 以内，且在分布外任务上表现出良好的泛化能力，显著优于传统的静态模型或启发式方法。

Conclusion: L2A 框架成功证明了在大语言模型推理中，通过预算感知策略动态调整计算资源是可行的，能够在不同资源约束下保持模型性能的鲁棒性，从而克服了静态模型在动态云环境下的局限性。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) inference is typically deployed under a static resource assumption, where models execute a fixed computational graph regardless of the runtime environment. However, real-world cloud infrastructure is inherently dynamic, characterized by fluctuating availability (e.g., spot instance preemption) and tiered Quality-of-Service requirements. In such volatile settings, static models are inflexible: they either crash under resource constraints or waste compute on redundant operations. To bridge this gap, we propose Learning to Allocate (L2A), an end-to-end framework for resource-adaptive inference. Unlike prior methods that condition only on input difficulty, we formulate inference as a constrained allocation problem conditioned on both the input and the runtime resource budget itself. We introduce lightweight, budget-conditioned and input-aware gating networks integrated into the LLM. These gates are trained via a unified objective that jointly optimizes task performance, logical consistency, and resource costs along three axes matching how real-world dynamics manifest: layer skipping for memory and depth pressure, head pruning for throughput contention, and reasoning-token reduction for latency tightening. This lets the model learn a budget-aware policy beyond input difficulty alone: it adaptively configures its computational footprint with respect to real-time resource dynamics, maximizing reasoning depth when resources permit while enforcing strict frugality when budgets tighten. A single L2A model traces the entire compute-accuracy Pareto frontier on Llama-3-8B and Qwen-3-4B: at up to 34% realized layer sparsity, it stays within 0.6% of the dense baseline on GSM8K, with the same gap holding zero-shot on out-of-distribution tasks, while every static or heuristic baseline requires a separately tuned model and still drops by 5-10% at comparable inference time.

</details>


### [46] [From Bootstrapping to Sequence Modeling: A Unified Generative Framework for Personalized Landing-Page Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27865)
*Fan Li,Chang Meng,Jiaqi Fu,Shuchang Liu,Tianke Zhang,Xueliang Wang,Xiaoqiang Feng,Yongqi Liu,Kaiqiao Zhan*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对个性化落地页导航任务，本文提出了一种基于决策Transformer的序列建模框架GLAN，通过整合全局消费动态建模与局部细粒度反馈监督，克服了传统强化学习方案在处理复杂用户行为序列时的缺陷，显著提升了用户活跃度与留存表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决在线平台个性化落地页建模（PLPM）中，现有基于保守Q学习（CQL）的方法存在的问题：一是忽略了用户行为的非马尔可夫时间依赖性；二是基于TD学习的引导式训练在长周期延迟奖励下存在累积误差和信度分配困难。

Method: 提出GLAN（生成式落地页自适应导航器）框架，基于决策Transformer（Decision Transformer）构建。包含两个核心模块：1. L-RTG模块：捕捉用户日间跨度内的消费动态，提供全局指引；2. HRM模块：将会话级反馈分解为细粒度信号，实现局部精准监督。

Result: 在快手平台的在线实验中，GLAN显著提升了用户体验，日活跃用户数（DAU）增长了0.158%，用户生命周期价值（LT）增长了0.108%。

Conclusion: GLAN通过将个性化落地页建模视为序列建模任务，有效解决了传统强化学习框架在处理非马尔可夫依赖和长周期延迟奖励时的局限性，为在线平台优化用户导航体验提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Modern online platforms increasingly adopt multi-page architectures to accommodate diverse user needs. On these platforms, page navigation (the process of directing users to specific functional pages upon app entry) serves as a critical gateway that shapes user's first impression and significantly influences subsequent engagement. To optimize this process, Kuaishou formulated the task of Personalized Landing Page Modeling (PLPM) and proposed KLAN, a reinforcement learning framework built upon Conservative Q-Learning (CQL). However, CQL-based approaches suffer from two fundamental limitations: (1) the Markov assumption fails to capture the strong non-Markovian temporal dependencies inherent in real-world user behaviors, and (2) TD learning with bootstrapping incurs severe cumulative errors and credit assignment difficulties under delayed rewards, particularly in long-horizon settings where users enter the app multiple times daily. To address these limitations, we propose GLAN (Generative Landing-page Adaptive Navigator), a sequence modeling framework built on Decision Transformer to tackle PLPM from a unified global-local perspective. Specifically, GLAN incorporates two key modules. First, we design the L-RTG module that captures users' inter-day consumption dynamics to provide accurate global guidance for all page assignments within a day. Furthermore, we propose the HRM module that decomposes session-level feedback into fine-grained signals, enabling precise local supervision for each page assignment. Extensive online experiments conducted on the Kuaishou platform demonstrate the effectiveness of GLAN, achieving +0.158\% and +0.108\% improvements on Daily Active Users (DAU) and user Lifetime (LT) respectively.

</details>


### [47] [An LLM-Powered Semantic Alignment Framework for Journal Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27930)
*Yanglin Yan,Zicheng Xie,Tianchen Gao,Rui Pan,Hansheng Wang*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于大语言模型（LLM）的零样本期刊推荐框架，通过直接对比论文内容与期刊范围的语义对齐，实现了准确、稳定且具有可解释性的学术期刊推荐，解决了传统推荐方法在通用性和可解释性上的不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的期刊推荐方法通常依赖于有监督学习模型、人工特征工程或历史交互数据，这些方法在通用性（generalizability）和可解释性（interpretability）方面存在局限。研究者旨在通过利用 LLM 的语义理解能力，构建一种无需训练即可工作的期刊推荐系统。

Method: 提出了一种基于大语言模型的语义对齐框架，将期刊推荐转化为手稿内容与期刊范围描述之间的语义匹配问题。该方法直接利用文章标题、摘要、关键词及候选期刊信息进行推理，无需针对特定任务进行模型训练。实验使用 DeepSeek-V3 模型，并评估了引入参考文献信息对推荐性能的影响。

Result: 在包含49个统计学及相关领域期刊的23,609篇文章数据集上，该框架的 Top-3、Top-5 和 Top-10 推荐准确率分别达到了 40.23%、53.67% 和 70.05%。此外，引入参考文献信息能有效提升推荐效果，且推荐过程具有高度稳定性（Top-5 Jaccard 相似度平均为 84%），并能生成可解释的推理说明。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了利用大语言模型（LLM）实现零样本（training-free）期刊推荐的可行性与有效性。该方法不仅在推荐准确率上表现优异，还具备高度的可解释性与稳定性，为学术信息系统中的决策支持提供了一种 scalable（可扩展）的新范式。

Abstract: Journal recommendation is an important task in scholarly information systems. Existing approaches typically rely on supervised learning models, manually engineered features, or historical interaction data, which may limit their generalizability and interpretability. We propose an LLM-powered semantic alignment framework that formulates journal recommendation as a semantic matching problem between manuscript content and journal scope descriptions. The framework enables large language models (LLMs) to infer journal suitability directly from article titles, abstracts, keywords, and candidate journal information without task-specific training. Experiments are conducted using DeepSeek-V3 on a dataset of 23,609 articles from 49 journals in statistics and related fields. The proposed framework achieves Top-3, Top-5, and Top-10 accuracies of 40.23\%, 53.67\%, and 70.05\%, respectively. Additional analyses show that incorporating reference information generally improves recommendation performance and that recommendations remain highly stable across repeated runs, with an average Top-5 Jaccard similarity of 84\%. The framework also generates interpretable reasoning outputs that provide insights into the recommendation process. These findings demonstrate the potential of LLMs as a training-free and scalable paradigm for journal recommendation and scholarly decision support.

</details>


### [48] [Listwise Explanation of Embedding-Based Rankings via Semantic Chunk Grouping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27980)
*Hyunkyu Kim,Yeeun Yoo,Youngjun Kwak*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出ChunkGroupSHAP方法，解决了现有解释方法无法有效归因稠密检索器的问题；研究证明解释单元的粒度应根据检索器模型特性及数据结构进行动态选择。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的列表式解释方法往往将排名归因于孤立的词汇，而稠密嵌入检索器（Dense Rankers）依赖的是上下文层面的句子或段落表示。这种“特征单元不匹配”导致词级归因过于碎片化，无法准确解释稠密检索器的行为。

Method: 提出了一种名为ChunkGroupSHAP的列表式Shapley解释方法。该方法将文档中语义相关的文本块（Chunks）聚类为共享的跨文档特征。通过对这些特征组进行掩码（Masking）操作，在保持列表式解释框架的同时，实现了与稠密模型表示粒度更匹配的归因分析。

Result: 在MS MARCO、FinanceBench、AILACaseDocs和FinQA等数据集上的实验表明：对于词法检索（如BM25），词级特征解释效果最好；对于稠密检索器，语料库层面的分组特征更优；而对于异构网页检索，查询局部（Query-local）分组最为有效。

Conclusion: 解释单元的选择应取决于检索器的表示粒度（词级或语义块级）以及检索语料库的结构。ChunkGroupSHAP通过将语义相关的文本块聚类，弥合了列表式解释方法与稠密检索器表示之间的粒度不匹配问题，提供了更具语义连贯性的归因结果。

Abstract: Dense embedding rankers score documents through contextual sentence- and passage-level representations. Yet many listwise explanation methods still attribute rankings to isolated words. This feature-unit mismatch leaves word-level features too fragmented for dense semantic ranking. We introduce ChunkGroupSHAP, a listwise Shapley method that clusters semantically related chunks into shared cross-document features. Masking a group perturbs all documents with related evidence, attributing rankings at a granularity closer to dense representations while preserving the listwise setup. Our findings across MS MARCO, FinanceBench, AILACaseDocs, and FinQA with E5 rankers and BM25 show that the best explanation unit is setting-dependent: word features for lexical BM25, corpus-level groups for dense rankers, and query-local grouping for heterogeneous web retrieval. Feature units should thus follow both the ranker's representational granularity and the structure of the retrieved corpus.

</details>


### [49] [Fast and Feasible: Permutation-based Constrained Reranking for Revenue Maximization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28059)
*Svetlana Shirokovskikh,Anastasiia Soboleva,Ekaterina Solodneva,Aleksandr Katrutsa,Roman Loginov,Egor Samosvat*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对电商搜索结果的广告重排序问题，本文提出了一种名为PermR的轻量级置换算法，在保障搜索相关性的前提下，有效提升了平台广告营收，并成功应用于超大规模在线系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在电商平台中，如何有效提升付费推广产品的曝光率（增加营收）的同时，又能保持搜索结果的相关性并避免损害用户体验，是当前排序系统面临的关键平衡挑战。由于精确求解ILP的计算开销过大，难以满足线上实时服务的延迟要求，因此需要开发更高效的近似方案。

Method: 1. 将重排序问题建模为整数线性规划（ILP），在最大化广告营收的同时，对相关性等指标施加约束；
2. 提出名为“PermR”的轻量级置换近似算法：通过对搜索结果中相邻项目进行交换，逐步优化目标函数或修复违反的约束。

Result: 1. 离线实验显示，PermR达到了最优ILP方案约63%的收益提升，且完全符合各项约束；
2. 在处理超过5600万次查询的14天在线A/B测试中，该算法成功将平台营收提升了2%，并满足了生产环境的延迟要求。

Conclusion: 本文提出的PermR算法成功平衡了电商平台搜索结果的相关性与广告营收，在满足严格的性能约束前提下，证明了轻量级置换算法在处理大规模在线排序优化问题中的高效性与实用价值。

Abstract: Search and recommender systems have produced highly relevant search results. A natural next step in the development of such systems in e-commerce is to rerank these results to increase the platform's revenue from paid promotion products. However, maximizing revenue alone may degrade the user experience by reducing relevance or increasing fraud risk. To avoid this, we state the reranking problem as an integer linear program ($ILP$) that maximizes revenue subject to per-query constraints on other metrics, e.g., relevance. Since solving $ILP$ exactly for every query is slow for deployment to the online service, we propose a lightweight permutation-based reranking approximation algorithm PermR. At each step, the algorithm selects a pair of neighboring items and swaps them to either improve the objective or repair a violated constraint. We evaluate PermR across multiple categories of a large classified platform in offline and online settings. PermR achieves about 63\% of the ILP revenue improvement, within production latency limits, preserving all constraints. In a 14-day online A/B test over 56 million search queries, PermR increased revenue by $2$\%.

</details>

### [50] [AI-Model Network: Concept, Current State and Future](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27382)
*Li Zhetao,Zeng Xiyu,Wang Jianhui,Xiao Yong,Liu Zhongren,Wu Junru,Lai Junjie,Huang Jijun,Long Saiqin*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文针对大模型时代异构模型难以高效协同的瓶颈，借鉴互联网思想，提出了“全球人工智能模型网络”（AI-ModelNet），旨在通过模型间的互联互通与能力共享，构建协作推理的新范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大模型技术的快速发展，训练成本高昂及部署复杂等问题日益突出，推动了轻量化、私有化和领域专用模型的发展。然而，如何实现大量异构模型之间的高效交互与协作，已成为当前人工智能领域亟待解决的瓶颈问题。

Method: 论文提出了“全球人工智能模型网络”（AI-ModelNet）概念，构建了一套分层系统架构。该方法通过在不同人工智能模型之间建立协作路径，实现了异构模型间的互联、能力共享以及协同推理。作者通过开发原型系统并在多个应用场景中进行验证，证明了该框架的可行性。

Result: 论文构建了 AI-ModelNet 的理论框架与系统架构，并通过原型系统展示了该范式在实现模型互联与能力协作方面的可行性。实验结果表明，该架构能有效支撑不同模型间的协同工作，为解决碎片化模型生态的互联难题提供了有效方案。

Conclusion: AI-ModelNet 作为一个创新范式，能够有效解决异构模型间的交互与协作难题，为实现大模型生态的互联互通提供了切实可行的路径，是推动人工智能从“单一智能”迈向“群体智能”的关键架构。

Abstract: While the primary function of computers lies in computation and processing, the core value of the Internet is rooted in sharing and collaboration. Computers create the Internet, and the Internet empowers the value of computers. The rapid development of the Internet, cloud computing, and big data is pushing artificial intelligence into the era of large models (LMs). However, the practical application of LMs is currently hindered by high training costs and deployment complexities, driving a shift toward lightweight, private, and domain-specific models. With the rapid proliferation and wide distribution of heterogeneous models, enabling effective interaction and collaboration among them has emerged as a critical bottleneck that urgently needs to be addressed in LM development. Drawing inspiration from the development of the Internet, this paper proposes the concept, vision, and system architecture of world wide AI-model network (AI-ModelNet). It is a novel paradigm that achieves interconnection, capability sharing, and collaborative reasoning by establishing pathways between models. We first briefly review the current state of single-model and multi-model research. Subsequently, the systemic vision and hierarchical architecture of AI-ModelNet are articulated, followed by validation of the framework's feasibility through a prototype system and diverse application cases. Finally, key directions for future research are discussed preliminarily.

</details>


### [51] [When Does Personality Composition Matter for Multi-Agent LLM Teams?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27443)
*Aryan Keluskar,Amrita Bhattacharjee,Huan Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了“个性化提示”对大模型多智能体团队性能的影响，发现个性特征对结果的影响取决于任务结构：简单任务不受影响，但协作与谈判类任务的绩效会随个性操纵而显著波动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然已有研究表明个性化提示能改变大模型的沟通风格（例如低宜人性倾向于对抗性语言），但目前尚不明确这些行为变化如何客观影响不同类型任务的最终成果，因此需要系统性地探究个性特征对多智能体协作性能的影响。

Method: 研究人员通过对前沿大型语言模型（LLM）施加不同的个性特征提示（如宜人性水平），并在三种不同类型的任务中进行测试：结构化编程任务、开放式研究协作任务以及竞争性议价任务，对比分析了不同个性配置下多智能体团队的任务完成情况和沟通表现。

Result: 研究发现个性对任务结果的影响具有任务依赖性：在结构化编程任务中，低宜人性带来的语言风格转变对里程碑完成情况几乎没有影响；然而，在开放式研究协作和竞争性议价任务中，同样的个性操作会导致任务性能显著下降。

Conclusion: 大模型的个性化提示虽然能显著改变其语言沟通风格，但其对任务结果的影响取决于任务的结构性质。在目标明确的结构化任务中，个性影响较小；而在需要协作或策略互动的任务中，不当的个性设置会显著降低系统性能。这对多智能体系统的设计提出了重要的约束建议。

Abstract: Personality prompting shapes how large language models communicate, yet whether these behavioral shifts affect objective task outcomes remains under-explored. Prior work shows that agents prompted with low agreeableness produce adversarial language, while those prompted with high agreeableness become cooperative, but the relationship between communication style and task performance has not been systematically examined across multiple domains. In this work, we investigate whether personality composition matters for multi-agent team performance by manipulating personality traits across frontier LLMs on three task domains: structured coding, open-ended research collaboration, and competitive bargaining. We find that personality effects depend critically on task structure. In coding tasks, low agreeableness leads to large communication shifts that have little effect on milestone completion. In open-ended collaboration and bargaining, the same manipulation substantially degrades performance. We discuss implications for multi-agent system design and the limits of personality manipulation.

</details>


### [52] [Internalizing the Future: A Unified Agentic Training Paradigm for World Model Planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27483)
*Xuan Zhang,Zhijian Zhou,Lingfeng Qiao,Yulei Qin,Ke Li,Xing Sun,Xiaoyu Tan,Chao Qu,Yuan Qi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对大模型智能体缺乏长时程规划能力的问题，本研究提出了一种三阶段训练框架，通过赋予模型内部世界模型和预测评估能力，使其能够像人类一样在行动前进行“假设性”推演。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LLM智能体在长时程任务中大多处于“反应式”，缺乏人类在行动前进行“假设性（what-if）”推理的能力，且现有的直接微调方法往往导致表面上的模仿而非真正的预测基础。

Method: 提出了一种三阶段训练范式：(1) 世界模型智能体中途训练 (WM-AMT)：注入潜在的预测能力；(2) 格式诱导微调 (FE-SFT)：将预测能力结构化；(3) 前瞻条件强化学习 (FC-RL)：校准和优化生成的模拟结果。模型通过自回归方式生成“前瞻状态推演”和“计划条件的成功估计（文本化Q值）”来实现推理。

Result: 在搜索和数学推理任务中，该方法持续优于其他基线训练方法，证明了其在实现有根据、经校准的前瞻性规划方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，通过“先能力、后结构”的三阶段训练范式，可以让大语言模型智能体具备真实且经过校准的内部世界模型能力，从而克服纯反应式决策的局限，显著提升在长时程任务中的表现。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents have demonstrated strong capability in sequential decision-making, yet they remains fundamentally reactive in long-horizon tasks. Unlike humans who employ "what-if" reasoning to evaluate potential plans before commitment, standard agents lack an internal world model to simulate future outcomes. Therefore, we propose to internalize future-aware planning by training a single autoregressive model to verbalize both a prospective state rollout and a plan-conditioned success estimate-a textual analogue of the Q-value. Crucially, we identify a format-capability gap: simply fine-tuning agents on look-ahead traces during post-training leads to superficial mimicry of foresight without genuine predictive grounding. To bridge this gap, we introduce a three-stage training paradigm: (i) World Model Agentic Mid-Training (WM-AMT) to inject latent predictive capabilities into the policy; (ii) Format-Eliciting SFT (FE-SFT) to structure this injected capability; and (iii) Foresight-Conditioned Reinforcement Learning (FC-RL) to refine the calibration and utility of the generated simulations. Evaluated on search and mathematical reasoning tasks, our approach consistently outperforms other training baselines. Our results demonstrate that effective internal world modeling in LLM agents requires a capability-first training pipeline to achieve grounded and calibrated foresight.

</details>


### [53] [Odyssey: Constructing Verifiable Local Truth-Preserving Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27593)
*Sridhar Mahadevan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ODYSSEY 是一个利用范畴论构建可验证基础模型的框架，通过将知识封装为可组合的“铸造厂”（Foundries），并利用 Kan 扩展进行形式化整合与验证，实现了具备逻辑严谨性和局部真值保持特性的智能系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的基础模型缺乏透明度、验证机制及局部真值保持能力，难以在复杂、严谨的决策场景（如科研、金融、制度分析）中可靠应用。作者旨在构建一种能够将知识、论证与模型更新逻辑有机结合的范畴论架构，以实现可信、可溯源的知识模型。

Method: 提出名为 ODYSSEY 的范畴论框架，利用“铸造厂”（foundry）作为构建块，通过左 Kan 扩展（Left Kan Extension）进行知识整合，利用右 Kan 扩展（Right Kan Extension）强制执行一致性、胶合规则和论证条件；同时引入 Foundry SQL (FSQL) 进行数据查询，并采用 TICKET 认证机制确保外部模型的合规接入。

Result: ODYSSEY 框架已完全实现并通过多领域测试，验证了其在领域构建、工件回放、层析诊断、基于 Toulmin 模型的局部 LLM 审查及因果声明提取等方面的有效性，能够跨异构来源进行高效的知识管理与验证。

Conclusion: ODYSSEY 框架证明了基于范畴论的组合式方法能够有效地构建可验证、局部真值保持的基础模型。通过将知识组织为“铸造厂”（foundries），该研究不仅提升了模型的可解释性和严谨性，还为处理异构数据源和复杂推理任务提供了一套通用的数学化解决方案。

Abstract: We introduce a categorical framework called ODYSSEY for constructing verifiable, local truth-preserving foundation models as compositions of foundries: building-block architectural components that specify a cover of local contexts, local representation families, restriction maps, gluing rules, obstruction policies, update obligations, and human-facing views. A foundry is an organized sheaf of knowledge that carries within it an argumentation component. Concrete foundries are built from generic foundries such as evidence/argument, operational decision, institutional/financial, market meaning, scientific challenge, research-program, assistant-build, and evaluation-harness foundries. Universal Foundry Learning (UFL) formalizes foundry construction as a composition of left and right Kan extensions, with left Kan extension rolling local artifacts into candidate foundries and right Kan extension enforcing the restriction, gluing, obstruction, and argumentation conditions required for promotion. Foundry SQL (FSQL) is a small typed query surface for slicing maintained foundry artifacts that uses TICKET (Topos Integration using Causal Kan Extension Transformers) certification for admitting external or pre-built models into durable ODYSSEY state. ODYSSEY is fully implemented and tested across a wide spectrum of concrete foundries, showing that the same categorical machinery supports domain construction, artifact replay, sheaf diagnostics, grounded Toulmin/local-LLM scrutiny, residual-obstruction ledgers, and optimized TICKET-compatible causal-claim extraction across heterogeneous sources. This paper is to be presented as a 2.5 hour tutorial at ICML 2026. The tutorial home page is at https://bit.ly/4ajS0nA.

</details>


### [54] [DysLexLens: A Low-Resource LLM Framework for Analysing Dyslexic Learners Insights from Online Forums](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27619)
*Dana Rezazadegan,Atie Kia,Phongpadid Nandavong,Dominique Carlon,Jeremy Nguyen,Abhik Banerjee,James Marshall,Anthony McCosker,Yong-Bin Kang*

Abstract: Dyslexic learners increasingly use artificial intelligence (AI) tools to support reading, writing, organisation, and study-related tasks. However, their lived experiences with these tools remain largely underexamined. This paper proposes DysLexLens, a low-resource LLM framework, designed to analyse dyslexic learners experience with AI through online forum discussions. DysLexLens is designed as an end-to-end, evidence-traceable architecture which transforms noisy social media posts into a dictionary-driven corpora, provides knowledge-graph (KG)-based question reasoning, generates verifiable query responses, and enables response evaluation through quantitative and human-grounded assessment. DysLexLens has four key features. First, it employs a dictionary-driven filtering method to construct a more focused Reddit corpus on dyslexia and AI, filtering out noisy and weakly related posts to improve the relevance of data collected from low-resource forum contexts. Second, it integrates LLM-assisted semantic analysis with KG-based query reasoning to uncover meaningful patterns. Third, it has quantitative evaluation metrics (RAGAS and Query Robustness) to measure LLM-generated response performance. Fourth, it provides structured qualitative validation guidelines for assessing response quality, with a specific focus on hallucination and evidence alignment. We demonstrate the effectiveness of DysLexLens using dyslexia-related Reddit forum data and 30 questions. The results show its potential generalisability to other low-resource forum data contexts. DysLexLens, sample data, questions and evaluation results are available at Github to support reproducibility.

### [55] [MER-R1: Multimodal Emotion Reasoning via Slow-Fast Thinking Synergy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27652)
*Zhiyuan Han,Beier Zhu,Wenwen Tong,Chengwei Qin,Xinyi Wang,Jiayu Zhang,Jiangnan Chen,Hewei Guo,Dongchuan Ran,Lewei Lu,Xun Yang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文针对多模态情感识别中“显式推理不一定提升精度”的问题，提出了一种名为 MER-R1 的强化学习框架。通过解耦并协同“快思考”的召回优势与“慢思考”的精确优势，实现了预测性能的显著提升，使推理过程真正服务于识别准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究中，多模态情感识别（MER）引入显式推理虽然提高了可解释性，但并不总是能提升预测准确率；该研究旨在探讨“快思考”（直觉预测）与“慢思考”（深思熟虑）在推理过程中的差异，并寻找一种机制使其相互补充而非相互抵消。

Method: 提出了 MER-R1 强化学习框架，核心策略包括：1. 双目标解耦，将召回率（快思考）和精确率（慢思考）作为独立的优化信号同时进行训练；2. 快慢思考置信度校准，通过快思考的直觉对慢思考的输出进行校准，增强正确情感的权重并抑制错误项。

Result: 在 MER-UniBench 和 MME-Emotion 等基准测试中，MER-R1 达到了当前最优（SOTA）水平，且实验证实了所提出的快慢思考互补机制能显著减少优化过程中的方差干扰。

Conclusion: 通过将“快思考”的直觉召回能力与“慢思考”的精确过滤能力进行互补与解耦优化，MER-R1 框架有效地解决了推理过程中的方差干扰问题，证明了推理机制能够通过正确的优化策略真正赋能多模态情感识别任务。

Abstract: We find that explicit reasoning does not necessarily translate into better multimodal emotion recognition (MER) accuracy, even though it makes predictions more interpretable. Specifically, for reasoning-based MLLMs, fast thinking by triggering direct answers often outperforms slow thinking after deliberative reasoning. Our empirical analyses show that fast thinking improves recall with broader and more confident predictions, whereas slow thinking favors precision through conservative filtering of incorrect categories. Building on these insights, we propose MER-R1, a reinforcement learning framework that turns slow-fast complementarity into explicit optimization. Dual-objective disentanglement separates recall and precision into two optimization signals, allowing them to be jointly optimized rather than traded off against each other. Slow-fast confidence calibration further aligns the final slow-thinking answer with fast-thinking intuition, strengthening correct emotions while suppressing incorrect ones. In this way, MER-R1 unifies the recall-oriented intuition of fast thinking with the precision-oriented selectivity of slow thinking. We further provide theoretical justification for this synergy, showing that it mitigates variance-induced interference during optimization. Extensive experiments on MER-UniBench and MME-Emotion show that MER-R1 achieves state-of-the-art performance and makes reasoning genuinely benefit emotion recognition.

ToE integrates a reinforcement learning-driven multi-source retrieval agent, an evidence evaluation agent, and an argument tree aggregation algorithm to iteratively decompose, retrieve, and verify claims through an explainable evidence chain. We further provide a theoretical analysis of the retrieval process, deriving a formal error bound that guarantees the learned policy converges to a neighborhood of the information-theoretically optimal policy. ### [58] [Understanding Rollout Error in Graph World Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27780)
*Xinyuan Song,Zekun Cai*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文针对图结构环境中的世界模型长程推演误差问题，提出了 Error-Aware GWM 框架，通过理论界限分析与正则化策略，有效解决了复杂图结构下的预测发散与规划性能下降问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的世界模型多针对向量或图像数据，难以应对复杂的图结构（如智能体、工具、技能及其依赖关系）。在图设置中，局部预测误差会通过拓扑结构传播，特别是在图结构本身随时间演化时，会导致更严重的长程推演偏差。因此，需要研究如何控制图世界模型中的长程推演误差。

Method: 1. 构建了统一的固定边与动态边图世界模型（GWM）框架；2. 推导出图值推演界限（graph-valued rollout bounds），区分了拓扑结构引起的误差放大与模型本身的预测误差；3. 提出联合节点-边算子用于处理动态边推演；4. 引入误差感知策略（Error-Aware GWM），结合谱正则化、推演一致性约束及关键节点加权来控制长程发散。

Result: 实验表明，随着推演步长的增加，未经处理的 GWM 会出现显著的误差积累与规划遗憾。Error-Aware GWM 能够有效抑制长程发散，同时保持较高的预测精度。研究还指出，对于结构动态演化的场景，动态边训练是必不可少的；而在静态或稀疏预测任务中，专业化的图模型可能更具优势。

Conclusion: 本文提出的 Error-Aware GWM 有效缓解了长程预测中的误差累积与发散问题，在动态图推演和智能体规划任务中展现了显著优势，明确了图世界模型在复杂结构演化场景下的应用价值。

Abstract: World models are often used for planning by rolling learned dynamics forward. Many planning environments, however, are not vectors or images; they are graphs of agents, tools, skills, routes, and dependencies. In these settings, a local prediction error may stay local or spread through the graph, and the failure mode changes again when edges are predicted rather than fixed. This paper studies long-horizon rollout error in Graph World Models (GWMs). We formulate a unified fixed-edge and dynamic-edge GWM framework with action nodes for node-, edge-, and graph-level decisions. We develop graph-valued rollout bounds that separate topology-induced amplification from model-induced amplification, and we introduce a joint node-edge operator for dynamic-edge rollouts. Guided by the analysis, we propose Error-Aware GWM, which combines spectral regularization, rollout consistency, and critical-node weighting. Across synthetic topologies and heterogeneous agent-graph testbeds, rollout error and planning regret grow with horizon, dynamic-edge training is needed when structure evolves, and Error-Aware GWM prevents long-horizon divergence while preserving prediction accuracy. Real-world graph benchmarks clarify the scope of GWMs: they are most useful for dynamic graph rollout and agent planning, while specialized graph models remain strong on static or sparse prediction tasks.

### [59] [Grounded Iterative Language Planning: How Parameterized World Models Reduce Hallucination Propagation in LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27806)
*Xinyuan Song,Zekun Cai*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 GILP 的新型规划框架，它融合了轻量级参数化模型的可靠性与 LLM 的推理灵活性，显著降低了语言智能体的幻觉率并提升了规划成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的语言智能体世界模型分为两类：基于代理（Agent-based）的模型推理灵活但容易产生难以量化的幻觉，而参数化（Parameterized）模型易于测量但规划能力较弱。研究旨在结合二者优势，解决语言智能体在复杂规划任务中频繁出现的幻觉和可靠性问题。

Method: 本文提出了“接地迭代语言规划”（Grounded Iterative Language Planning, GILP）。该方法使用一个小的参数化骨干网络来预测动作、状态变化、风险和价值，并将其与基于 API 的 LLM 智能体相结合。通过一个“一致性门控”（consistency gate）机制，当参数化模型与 LLM 的预测不一致时，触发 LLM 进行修订。此外，研究还引入了针对基于智能体的世界模型的“操作性幻觉度量”方法。

Result: 在真实 GPT-4o-mini 调用测试中，GILP 将幻觉状态率从 0.176 降低至 0.035。在模拟器消融实验中，该方法在仅增加约 22% LLM 调用次数的情况下，将任务成功率从 0.668 提升至 0.838。

Conclusion: GILP 方法通过结合参数化世界模型与大语言模型（LLM）的优势，有效地解决了智能体在规划过程中的幻觉问题。该研究证明了将轻量级、可预测的参数化模型与灵活的 LLM 结合，是提升智能体规划任务性能与可靠性的有效途径。

Abstract: World models for language agents come in two useful forms. An agent-based world model calls an LLM API and reasons flexibly in language, but its errors appear as hallucinated state changes that are hard to score with ordinary regression losses. A parameterized world model is a trained transition predictor; its errors are easier to measure with quantities such as NodeMSE, delta accuracy, and validity accuracy, but it is usually weaker as a standalone planner. We compare these two families on four graph-structured planning benchmarks and introduce operational hallucination metrics for the agent-based case. The comparison motivates \textbf{Grounded Iterative Language Planning} (GILP), which trains only a small parameterized backbone and combines it with API-based agent reasoning. The backbone supplies valid actions, predicted state deltas, risk, and value; the LLM drafts an action and imagined delta; and a consistency gate asks for revision when the two disagree. On real GPT-4o-mini calls, GILP reduces hallucinated-state rate from 0.176 to 0.035. In calibrated simulator ablations, it raises success from 0.668 to 0.838 while adding only ~22% extra LLM calls.

</details>


### [60] [ATOD: Annealed Turn-aware On-policy Distillation for Multi-turn Autonomous Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27814)
*Qitai Tan,Zefang Zong,Yang Li,Peng Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ATOD通过融合模仿学习的快速收敛特性与强化学习的奖励优化机制，利用退火调度和动态加权，实现了对小语言模型代理训练效率与性能上限的双重提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解决小型语言模型代理在处理长程交互任务时，面临模仿学习（OPD）性能天花板和强化学习（RL）早期学习效率低的两难问题。

Method: 提出了退火轮次感知在线蒸馏（ATOD）算法，包含两个核心机制：1. 退火OPD-RL调度，前期通过OPD快速模仿教师，后期逐步增强RL以突破性能上限；2. 轮次级不确定性加权（T-DUR），通过软性放大高价值交互轮次的权重，增强长轨迹中的监督信息。

Result: 在ALFWorld、WebShop和Search-QA基准测试中，ATOD表现优异，平均成功率较OPD提升3.03个百分点，较GRPO提升23.62个百分点，并超越了教师模型本身（提升2.16个百分点）。

Conclusion: ATOD算法有效结合了模仿学习与强化学习的优势，通过退火调度和差异化加权策略，解决了小模型在长程交互任务中训练效率低和性能瓶颈的问题，显著提升了代理模型的最终表现。

Abstract: Training small language-model agents for long-horizon interactive tasks requires both fast imitation and reward-driven improvement. On-policy distillation (OPD) provides dense teacher guidance and typically improves rapidly in the early stage, but its gains saturate once the student approaches the teacher, limiting the final performance ceiling. Reinforcement learning (RL) directly optimizes environment rewards and encourages exploratory improvement toward a higher reward-defined ceiling, but sparse and delayed feedback makes early-stage learning much less efficient than OPD. In this paper, we propose ATOD (Annealed Turn-aware On-policy Distillation), a hybrid online distillation algorithm that explicitly exploits this complementarity. (1) ATOD uses an annealed OPD-RL schedule: OPD dominates early training to approach teacher-level behavior, while RL is gradually strengthened to drive reward-based exploration. (2) ATOD introduces Turn-level Disagreement-Uncertainty Reweighting (T-DUR), which softly amplifies high-utility turns and improves dense supervision in long trajectories. Experiments on ALFWorld, WebShop, and Search-QA show that ATOD consistently outperforms competing post-training baselines: across the three student sizes, ATOD improves average success rate by 3.03 points over OPD and 23.62 points over GRPO, while surpassing the corresponding teacher models by 2.16 points.

</details>

TL;DR: 针对具身智能体难以在完成任务时主动遵守隐性社会规范的问题，本文提出了NormAct基准测试，并开发了NormPerceptor提示生成器，有效提升了模型在复杂场景下的社会规范遵守能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）在具身环境中虽然能完成显性目标，但往往忽略了现实社会中存在的隐性行为规范。目前缺乏能够评估模型在行动序列中主动推断并应用这些隐含社会约束能力的基准，导致模型在社会交互任务中表现不佳。

Method: 1. 构建了NormAct基准测试：将隐性社会规范嵌入普通任务中，评估模型在不接受显式指令情况下对规范的遵守能力。 2. 提出了NormPerceptor：一个上下文相关的提示生成器，旨在规划前推断并激活场景相关的社会规范，将其转化为行动约束。

Result: 1. 现有先进MLLMs（如GPT-4o, Claude 3.5, Gemini 1.5 Pro等）在实现显性目标方面表现尚可（67.3%），但在遵守隐性规范上表现极差（仅26.4%）。 2. 实验证明差距源于模型无法在上下文中激活和定位相关规范。 3. 使用NormPerceptor后，模型的整体任务成功率从24.2%显著提升至46.7%。

Conclusion: 本文强调了具身智能体不仅需要完成显性目标，还必须具备主动感知隐性社会规范并在复杂场景中将其转化为行动约束的能力。通过NormPerceptor引入上下文感知的提示机制，能有效缩小模型在规范执行上的差距，为构建更具社会责任感和适应性的具身智能体提供了重要研究方向。

Abstract: Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) are increasingly deployed as embodied planners in egocentric environments, where task success requires not only achieving instructed goals but also acting in socially appropriate ways. While explicit goals may render certain actions optimal, implicit social norms often impose hidden constraints. Existing evaluations typically focus on explicit goal achievement or direct norm knowledge, seldom assessing whether planners can infer and apply these hidden constraints within action sequences. We introduce NormAct, a benchmark for embodied social-norm interactions that evaluates plans on Goal Achievement, Norm Compliance, and overall Task Success. NormAct uniquely embeds hidden norms within ordinary tasks, testing whether models can realize them without explicit instruction. Experiments with state-of-the-art MLLMs (GPT-5.4, Claude Opus 4.7, Gemini 3 Pro) reveal a significant gap: models achieve explicit goals in 67.3\% of cases, but comply with hidden norms in only 26.4\%. Cue-condition experiments indicate that this gap stems not from a lack of general social knowledge, but from challenges in activating and grounding relevant norms in context. To address this, we propose NormPerceptor, a context-conditioned cue generator that infers scene-relevant norms prior to planning, increasing Task Success from 24.2\% to 46.7\%. Our results underscore the importance of enabling embodied agents to proactively detect hidden norms, ground them in visual evidence, and integrate them as action-planning constraints. Our benchmark is publicly available at https://huggingface.co/datasets/Caleb196x/NormAct.

### [62] [Verifiable Geometry Problem Solving: Solver-Driven Autoformalization and Theorem Proposing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27926)
*Can Li,Ting Zhang,Junbo Zhao,Hua Huang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了SD-GPS框架，通过将符号求解器深度整合进自动形式化与定理推导过程，解决了几何问题求解中形式化与执行脱节、推导逻辑受限的问题，显著提升了机器解决几何证明问题的能力与准确性。

Method: 提出了名为SD-GPS的求解器驱动框架，核心创新点在于：1. 求解器驱动的自动形式化，利用强化学习将符号求解器的可执行性作为训练信号；2. 验证式定理提案，设计了一个具有死锁感知能力的智能体，通过符号验证确保所提出的辅助引理的正确性。

Result: 在Geometry3K和PGPS9K数据集上的实验结果表明，SD-GPS在标准补全、多项选择及跨模态引用等多种任务中，均优于现有的多模态大模型（MLLM）、神经方法及神经符号方法。

Abstract: Geometry Problem Solving have increasingly adopt the neuro-symbolic paradigm, combining neural intuition with symbolic rigor. However, current frameworks suffer from severe bottlenecks in two core stages: autoformalization, which treats multimodal translation as a static task decoupled from downstream solver compatibility, and theorem prediction, where solvers frequently hit a deductive impasse due to fixed rule libraries. To address these, we propose SD-GPS, a solver-driven framework that treats the symbolic solver as an execution oracle throughout both formalization and deduction. First, Solver-Driven Autoformalization unifies supervised formal-language adaptation and solvability-guided reinforcement learning into a single module built on QwenVL3-2B, making executability the central training signal. Second, Verified Theorem Proposing introduces an impasse-aware agent that proposes local auxiliary lemmas from current proof states, ensuring soundness by filtering all proposals through symbolic verification. Empirical evaluations on Geometry3K and PGPS9K demonstrate that SD-GPS consistently outperforms existing MLLM, neural, and neuro-symbolic methods across standard completion, multiple-choice, and cross-modal reference regimes, proving that closing the loop between multimodal perception and symbolic execution significantly improves geometric reasoning, offering profound insights into how neural agents can be grounded by formal systems to achieve verifiable problem-solving capabilities.

### [63] [RelBall: Relation Ball with Quaternion Rotation for Knowledge Graph Completion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27967)
*Yike Liu,Peijia Xie,Chao He,Huiling Zhu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对知识图谱补全中复杂关系模式和语义层次建模的挑战，本文提出了 RelBall 模型，通过模量变换建模层次，并通过尾部中心球结构支持各种基数关系，有效提升了链路预测能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有知识图谱补全模型（如 RotatE, Rotate3D）在处理非交换性组合模式、语义层次结构以及复杂基数关系（如一对多）时存在明显的局限性。

Method: 提出了 RelBall 模型：1. 引入模量变换（modulus transformation），通过模量的大小映射概念的抽象程度（抽象概念模量小，具体实例模量大）以建模语义层次；2. 引入尾部中心关系球（tail-centric relation ball）机制，有效建模各种基数关系（1-to-1, 1-to-N, N-to-1, N-to-N）。

Result: 实验结果表明，RelBall 在多个基准数据集上取得了优于或竞争于主流基线的知识图谱补全性能，同时具备更好的可解释性和对复杂关系模式的覆盖能力。

Conclusion: RelBall 通过引入模量变换和尾部中心关系球，成功克服了现有模型在处理非交换性组合、语义层次结构及复杂基数关系方面的局限性，在知识图谱补全任务中展现出卓越的表达能力和预测性能。

Abstract: Real-world knowledge graphs are often incomplete, lacking many valid facts. Knowledge Graph Completion (KGC) aims to predict missing links using known triples, thereby enhancing graph coverage. A key challenge is modeling diverse relational patterns such as symmetry, antisymmetry, inversion, composition and semantic hierarchy. Existing models such as RotatE can capture symmetric, antisymmetric, inverse, and commutative composition patterns, yet struggle with non-commutative composition. Rotate3D addresses this by introducing non-commutativity via three-dimensional rotations, but still fails to capture the semantic hierarchies prevalent in knowledge graphs. Moreover, both models cannot effectively model one-to-many relations. To overcome these limitations, we propose RelBall, which extends Rotate3D with two innovations. First, our model introduces modulus transformation to model hierarchies, driving abstract concepts toward smaller moduli and concrete instances toward larger ones. Second, it introduces a tail-centric relation ball to model one-to-one, one-to-many, many-to-one, and many-to-many relations. RelBall offers the following advantages: (1) coverage of all relational patterns, including the ones mentioned above; (2) an interpretable hierarchical representation where the modulus directly reflect semantic levels; (3) support for one-to-one, one-to-many, many-to-one, and many-to-many relations. Experiments on multiple datasets demonstrate RelBall's competitive link prediction performance against various baselines.

### [64] [Lifted Causal Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28024)
*Malte Luttermann,Tanya Braun,Ralf Möller,Marcel Gehrke*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 提出了参数化因果因子图（PCFGs）以在提升模型中整合因果知识，并定义了干预的正式语义；2. 设计了提升因果推断（LCI）算法，在提升层面直接计算因果效应；3. 进一步提出了部分有向参数化因果因子图（PD-PCFGs），以处理不完整的因果知识，并扩展了LCI算法的适用范围。

Conclusion: 该研究通过引入PCFG和PD-PCFG模型以及LCI算法，证明了提升推理（Lifted Inference）能够有效应用于关系领域中的因果推断，在保持精确性的前提下，显著降低了计算复杂度，并增强了模型在处理不完全因果知识时的灵活性。

Abstract: Lifted inference exploits indistinguishabilities in probabilistic graphical models by using a representative for indistinguishable objects, thereby speeding up query answering while maintaining exact answers. In this article, we show how lifting can be applied to efficiently compute causal effects in relational domains. More specifically, we introduce parametric causal factor graphs (PCFGs) to incorporate causal knowledge in lifted models and give a formal semantics of interventions therein. We further present the Lifted Causal Inference (LCI) algorithm to compute causal effects on a lifted level, thereby drastically speeding up causal inference compared to propositional inference, e.g., in causal Bayesian networks. In addition, we present partially directed parametric causal factor graphs (PD-PCFGs) as a generalisation of PCFGs to handle partial causal knowledge and extend LCI to perform lifted causal inference in a PD-PCFG, thereby extending the applicability of lifted causal inference to a broader range of models requiring less prior knowledge about causal relationships.

### [66] [Ontology-Guided Evidence Path Inference for Multi-hop Knowledge Graph Question Answering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28076)
*Yongxue Shan,Meihan Wu,Cundi Fang,Jie Peng,Xiaodong Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: OPI是一种本体引导的KGQA框架，通过关系中心本体图与双向检索机制，在大幅压缩搜索空间的同时，显著提高了复杂问题推理的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多跳知识图谱问答（KGQA）方法多依赖以主题为中心的扩展，导致搜索空间因噪声路径迅速膨胀，且检索到的路径往往难以满足复杂问题的语义约束。

Method: 提出了一种基于本体引导的证据路径推理框架（OPI）：1. 构建关系中心本体图以捕获关系约束；2. 引入双向检索机制，结合主题侧前缀扩展与答案侧末跳匹配，减少噪声路径；3. 采用迭代细化策略，根据问题上下文重新评估并过滤不相关证据。

Abstract: Knowledge graph question answering (KGQA) aims to answer natural-language questions by reasoning over structured facts. Existing multi-hop KGQA methods mainly rely on topic-centered expansion, which faces two key challenges: the search space rapidly grows with noisy mixed-type paths, and retrieved paths may fail to satisfy the semantic constraints of complex questions. To address these challenges, we propose OPI, an ontology-guided evidence path inference framework for multi-hop KGQA. OPI introduces a relation-centric ontology graph to capture the head-tail type constraints of relations, providing a compact interface for answer-side constraints. Based on this ontology graph, OPI first introduces a bidirectional retrieval mechanism by mapping the predicted answer type to compatible final-hop relations and combining topic-side prefix expansion with answer-side final-hop matching, thereby suppressing noisy mixed-type expansion. OPI further adopts an iterative refinement strategy to reassess retrieved paths and candidate answers under the question context, filtering type-compatible but question-irrelevant evidence for more reliable answer prediction. Experiments on WebQSP, CWQ, and MetaQA show that OPI substantially reduces the search space, improves Hit@1/F1 by 4.6/5.0 points on WebQSP and 8.9/3.3 points on CWQ over the strongest prior results, and achieves near-saturated Hit@1 on MetaQA with the retrieval module alone.

### [68] [Tandem Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28166)
*Difan Jiao,Raghav Singhal,Robert West,Ashton Anderson*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了串联强化学习（TRL），通过让资深模型在训练中与冻结的初级模型协作生成推理内容，成功解决了传统强化学习推理过程漂移严重、可读性差的问题，实现了推理能力与协作兼容性的平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）虽提升了模型的推理能力，但往往会导致推理过程出现可读性差、语言混合等“特质化”漂移，使得人类或较弱的模型难以理解其逻辑。串联训练范式虽旨在解决该问题，但在长链式思维的现代RLVR工作流中的扩展性和有效性尚未得到充分验证。

Method: 提出串联强化学习（Tandem Reinforcement Learning, TRL）。在该方法中，由一个资深模型（senior）和一个冻结的初级模型（junior）随机交替协作生成推理链，并应用标准的组相对策略优化（GRPO）损失函数对资深模型进行训练。通过这种机制，资深模型被迫学习如何生成初级模型更容易理解和跟随的推理路径。

Result: 在Qwen3-4B-Instruct模型和竞赛数学任务上的实验表明，TRL在保持与传统GRPO相当的独立推理能力的同时，实现了三项显著优势：提高了与初级模型的交接鲁棒性，减少了对初级模型分布的偏离，并增强了推理链对初级模型的可读性。

Conclusion: 串联强化学习（TRL）是一种有效的训练范式，能够在保持模型推理能力的同时，提升模型输出内容的可读性与协作鲁棒性。该研究证实了通过在训练中引入“资深模型”与“资深模型”的交替生成，可以解决强化学习中常见的推理过程漂移问题，为多模型协作及人机兼容的语言模型开发提供了重要路径。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has significantly improved the reasoning capability of large language models, reaching expert or even superhuman performance in domains such as competition math. However, whether weaker agents and humans can actually harness this capability is far less certain, with RLVR documented to drift reasoning toward idiosyncratic patterns such as poor readability and language mixing. Tandem training is a recently introduced paradigm that targets this compatibility problem: a trained, stronger senior co-generates each rollout with a frozen, weaker junior, and the two are rewarded as a team, so the senior is pushed to reason in ways the junior can follow. Yet this paradigm has so far been demonstrated only in proof-of-concept settings, leaving open whether it scales to the long chains of thought of the modern RLVR pipeline. In this work, we propose Tandem Reinforcement Learning (TRL), which carries the tandem training paradigm into RLVR. In TRL, the senior and a frozen junior alternate stochastically to co-generate the reasoning, the resulting generation is rewarded, and the standard GRPO loss is applied to the senior. Training Qwen3-4B-Instruct on competition math, we find that TRL matches vanilla GRPO on solo reasoning capability while three properties emerge together from the same rollout structure: stronger handoff robustness with the junior, reduced distributional drift from the junior, and a chain-of-thought more legible to the junior. Our results demonstrate a promising route for RLVR with practical payoffs in multi-model communication and human compatibility.

</details>


### [69] [Agent-Native Immune System: Architecture, Taxonomy, and Engineering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28270)
*Bo Shen,Lifeng Chang,Tianyuan Wei,Yunpeng Li,Feng Shi,Yichen Han,Peijie Gao,Shiyi Kuang,Xin Chang,Dehui Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对现有防御机制无法有效保护自主智能体的问题，本文提出了“智能体原生免疫系统（ANIS）”，通过将防御机制内嵌于智能体的认知循环中，实现了对运行期攻击的动态防御和持续免疫学习。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从静态聊天机器人到具备记忆、工具使用和多智能体协作的自主智能体的演进，大幅扩展了AI威胁领域。现有的防御机制（如边界安全和训练时对齐）独立于智能体的认知循环之外，导致智能体在运行期极易受到记忆投毒、工具链操纵等攻击。

Result: 提出了一种生物启发的内源性防御体系，证明了在智能体认知循环内直接集成防御机制的可行性，能够有效应对运行期劫持等复杂安全威胁，提升智能体的鲁棒性和动态防御能力。

Conclusion: 本文提出了Agent-Native Immune System (ANIS)，这是一种内嵌于智能体认知循环中的防御架构。它在理论上明确了模型对齐（静态宪法）与智能体免疫（动态执法）的区别，并指出未来需关注免疫协议标准化、评估指标（如自身免疫率）以及智能体生态中病原体与疫苗的共进化动力学。

Abstract: The transition from static chat bots to autonomous agents--equipped with persistent memory, tool-use protocols, and multi-agent collaboration--has fundamentally expanded the AI threat landscape. Current defense mechanisms, such as perimeter security and training-time alignment, remain external to the agent's active reasoning loop. Consequently, they fall short: a fully aligned agent remains highly vulnerable to runtime hijacking via memory poisoning, tool-chain manipulation, or multi-agent protocol attacks. To address this critical gap, we introduce the Agent-Native Immune System (ANIS), the first biologically inspired, endogenous defense architecture embedded directly within the agent's cognitive loop. Our framework presents four primary contributions. First, we design a six-layer Immune Tower (L0-L5), distinctly incorporating Barrier Immunity (L1) as a non-cognitive, physical-and-logical isolation layer. Second, we establish a unified taxonomy of Agent Viruses and Agent Vaccines, formalizing the critical distinction between superficial non-parametric defenses and robust parametric vaccines. Third, we conceptualize the Harness Triad--Meta, Self, and Auto--a self-monitoring, meta-cognitive automation backbone that drives Continual Immune Learning (CIL), enabling vaccines to dynamically adapt to novel threats. Finally, we establish a rigorous theoretical demarcation between model alignment and agent immunity: while alignment provides a static "constitutional" value foundation during training, ANIS serves as the dynamic "law enforcement" mechanism during runtime. We conclude by framing open challenges for the field, including immune protocol standardization, novel evaluation metrics such as the Autoimmunity Rate (false-positive intervention rate), and the co-evolutionary dynamics between pathogens and vaccines within collective intelligence ecosystems.

### [70] [OverFlowLight: Real-Time Gridlock Prevention and Traffic Signal Optimization for Urban Intersections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27381)
*Mingyuan Li,Boyang Huang,Tianqi Jiang,Chenpu Li,Chunyu Liu,Yang Li,Ruimin Li,Qiang Wu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 OverFlowLight，这是一个结合多模态感知和混合控制的交通信号控制框架，旨在通过实时检测溢出并动态调整信号相位，有效预防城市交通路口溢出及连锁拥堵，显著提升了通行效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的交通信号控制（TSC）算法多以最大化通行能力为目标，在高峰时段难以有效应对队列溢出，导致严重的交通拥堵、连锁式路口瘫痪及安全隐患。因此，需要一种能够主动预测并解决溢出的实时控制框架。

Method: 提出 OverFlowLight 框架：首先利用摄像头和雷达进行多模态感知以实时检测溢出；其次采用混合控制策略，即结合规则驱动的快速溢出干预与基于强化学习（RL）的长期效率优化，通过动态插入溢出相位来清理阻塞队列。

Result: 通过在三个主要城市的 43 个路口进行实地部署，结果表明该框架较现有基线方案将溢出事件减少了 60.4%，网络吞吐量提高了 18.2%，并显著降低了对人工调参的依赖。

Conclusion: OverFlowLight 是一种实用、可扩展且由数据驱动的框架，通过混合控制策略有效解决了城市交通中的溢出问题，为构建韧性强的智能交通系统提供了关键技术支撑。

Abstract: Queue overflow, a severe consequence of urban traffic congestion, occurs when vehicle queues exceed intersection capacity, obstructing upstream traffic and triggering cascading gridlocks. Prevailing traffic signal control (TSC) algorithms, primarily optimized for throughput, often fail to address overflow during peak hours, exacerbating congestion and creating safety hazards. We propose OverFlowLight, a real-time framework designed to preemptively resolve overflow and enhance overall TSC performance. It first introduces a mechanism to accurately detect overflow in real-time by leveraging multi-modal sensing from cameras and radars. Upon detection, it dynamically generates and inserts dedicated overflow phases into the signal cycle to clear the blocking queues. This is orchestrated by a hybrid control design that combines rapid rule-based overflow intervention with controller back ends such as reinforcement learning (RL) for longer-horizon efficiency. We conducted extensive real-world deployments of OverFlowLight across 43 intersections in three major cities. The framework demonstrates seamless integration with existing RL-based TSC agents, highlighting its modularity and practical applicability. Empirical results show that OverFlowLight reduces overflow incidents by 60.4% and increases network throughput by 18.2% compared to deployed baselines. Furthermore, it substantially diminishes the need for manual intervention common with expert-tuned signal plans. This work presents the first practical, scalable, and data-driven framework for actively preventing traffic gridlock, offering a crucial component for building resilient and efficient urban transportation systems. Our demonstration videos, codes and datasets are available at the anonymous URL, https://anonymous.4open.science/r/OverFlowLight-FBF9.

### [71] [RANSAC Scoring Done Right](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27385)
*James Pritts,Felix Seegräber,Kevin Köser*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种无需用户设定残差阈值的创新RANSAC评分方法，通过数学手段解析地消除了对内点尺度的依赖，不仅实现了自适应计算，还在各类基准测试中显著提升了鲁棒性和计算效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的RANSAC变体（如RANSAC, MSAC等）高度依赖用户设定的残差阈值参数，而该参数依赖于受污染数据中难以准确估计的内点尺度。作者旨在解决这一依赖性，消除人工调参的需求，并提高算法在不同数据量下的鲁棒性。

Method: 提出了基于共轭逆伽马先验分布的解析边缘化方法，将内点尺度从评分公式中剔除。该评分函数涵盖了从非信息Jeffreys先验到经验贝叶斯先验的范围，并利用“排序与扫描”（sort-and-sweep）算法将计算复杂度优化至O(N log N)。

Result: 在包含近7万对图像的基准测试中，该方法表现出色。即使在阈值校准不准的情况下依然保持稳定，在极少验证数据（仅两对）下即可达到接近最优的精度，且在数据匮乏时能自动加强先验正则化，整体性能优于现有的RANSAC, MSAC, GaU和MAGSAC。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种无需人工设定阈值参数的RANSAC评分方法。通过在贝叶斯框架下解析地边缘化内点尺度，该方法实现了对不同数据规模的自适应性，在鲁棒性和精度上均优于现有的主流算法，是RANSAC参数化问题上的重要突破。

Abstract: The most widely used RANSAC variants score candidate models by counting inliers or summing per-point scores that saturate beyond a residual threshold. Every such score requires a user-supplied parameter that is a function of the inlier scale, which must itself be estimated from contaminated data. We remove this dependence by reversing the usual order of inference: rather than estimating the scale and then scoring against it, we marginalize the inlier scale analytically in closed form under a conjugate Inverse-Gamma prior for a fixed inlier partition, then optimize over partitions. A single closed-form expression spans the non-informative Jeffreys limit and informative empirical-Bayes priors, so the same score adapts across data-rich and data-scarce regimes without any change to the algorithm. The proposed RANSAC score is the first in which the inlier scale is genuinely absent from the formula. The score admits O(N log N ) computation via sort-and-sweep. On a benchmark of nearly 70 000 image pairs spanning different two-view estimation problems and both engineered and learned feature pipelines, the proposed score exceeds the state of the art (RANSAC, MSAC, GaU, MAGSAC): it stays nearly flat under threshold miscalibration where baselines degrade, reaches near-optimal accuracy from as few as two validation pairs where baselines need ont he order of 100 times more,. and tightens its prior regularization as validation data grows scarce.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前时间序列基础模型（Foundation Models）虽在零样本预测方面展现出巨大潜力，但往往以孤立的包形式发布，接口碎片化且缺乏与现有主流工具库的互操作性，导致在实际生产流水线中集成和评估变得困难。

Method: 作者在 Darts 库中开发了一套统一的 FoundationModel 类集合，将 Chronos-2、TimesFM 2.5、TiRex 和 PatchTST-FM 等主流时间序列基础模型封装为具有标准化接口的模块，并简化了其与现有数据处理、回测及不确定性估计工具的集成路径。

Result: Darts 的用户现在只需修改模型名称即可在现有流水线中使用基础模型，或者将其用于零样本预测、微调、不确定性估计等复杂任务，无需处理繁琐的外部依赖或接口适配问题。

Conclusion: Darts 通过引入统一的 FoundationModel 类，成功弥合了前沿时序大模型与工业级数据处理流水线之间的鸿沟，使得开发者能够以极低的迁移成本，在统一框架下实现对不同基础模型的零样本预测、微调及评估，显著提升了时序分析工具的可用性与互操作性。

Abstract: Since its initial release in 2020, Darts has become a widely used open-source Python library for time series analysis. A series of foundation models have recently claimed accuracy improvements in zero-shot forecasting, promising a paradigm shift from training custom models to harnessing pre-trained general-purpose forecasters. Foundation models, however, are often released as isolated packages with fragmented interfaces and limited interoperability with common tooling, making joint evaluation and integration within complete pipelines difficult. In Darts, we developed a unified $\texttt{FoundationModel}$ class collection (Chronos-2, TimesFM 2.5, TiRex, PatchTST-FM) that provides standardized, full-cycle forecasting interfaces with minimal external dependencies for integrating foundation models into the ecosystem. Existing Darts pipelines can now use foundation models with only a name change; new pipelines can use them for zero-shot or fine-tuned forecasting, uncertainty estimation, and backtesting, combined with data processing and evaluation tooling, all within a unified framework.

### [73] [PairSAE: Mechanistic Interpretability from Pair Representations in Protein Co-Folding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27440)
*Giosue Migliorini,Aristofanis Rontogiannis,Grigori Guitchounts,Nicholas Franklin,Axel Elaldi,Olivia Viessmann*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对结构生物学模型（Pairformer）难以解释的问题，本文提出了 PairSAE 方法，通过 SVD 压缩和稀疏自编码技术，成功从复杂的成对表示中提取出可解释的生物学特征，且避免了传统方法带来的特征维度爆炸问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管结构生物学基础模型在结构预测和设计方面表现出色，但其内部潜空间特征的可解释性较差。传统的稀疏自编码器（SAE）直接应用于 Pairformer 架构的成对表示时，不仅会导致特征数量的二次方爆炸，还会掩盖分布在序列和成对表示中的联合概念，迫切需要一种更有效的特征提取方案。

Method: 研究人员提出了一种名为 PairSAE 的方法，旨在解决处理成对（pairwise）表示时的计算开销和特征难以解释的问题。该方法首先通过 N-mode 奇异值分解（SVD）将成对张量压缩为标记级（token-wise）的交互角色，随后利用稀疏自编码器（SAE）学习一套共享的标记级特征，并将这些特征解码回原始的序列和成对表示中。

Result: 在 PLINDER 蛋白质-配体复合物数据集上，PairSAE 学习到的特征表现出良好的可解释性，不仅能与 UniProt 注释良好对齐，还能有效预测 Boltz-2 的亲和力数值。这证明了该方法在保持结构语义的同时，成功提取出了具有生物学意义的内部特征。

Conclusion: PairSAE 有效弥合了结构生物学基础模型（如 Pairformer 架构）的高维潜空间与可解释结构概念之间的鸿沟，为理解生物分子模型的内部决策机制提供了一种有效且计算高效的方法。

Abstract: Foundation models for structural biology have achieved remarkable performance in predicting biomolecular structure and show promise for the design of proteins and small molecules. Yet understanding which internal features drive their outputs remains challenging. Standard sparse autoencoders (SAEs), effective on transformer-style sequence embeddings, do not transfer cleanly to pairformer-like architectures: naively operating on pairwise representations yields a quadratic blow-up of features and obscures concepts distributed jointly across sequence and pair representations.
  We introduce PairSAE, which summarizes pairwise tensors via an N-mode SVD into token-wise interaction roles, then uses a sparse autoencoder to learn a shared set of token-level features that decode into both sequence and pair representations. Evaluated on Boltz-2 activations for PLINDER protein-ligand complexes, PairSAE yields interpretable features that align with UniProt annotations and predict Boltz-2 affinity values. These results indicate that PairSAE links the latent space of foundation models for structural biology to interpretable structural concepts, clarifying what the model "knows" while avoiding pairformer-induced pitfalls that limit conventional SAEs.

### [74] [Learning in Markovian bandits with non-observable states and constrained decision epochs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27448)
*Thomas Hira,Victor Boone,Urtzi Ayesta,Ina Maria Verloop*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了状态不可观测的马尔可夫多臂老虎机问题，引入了“自退化”模型并设计了UCB-NOM算法。研究发现，尽管状态不可观测导致在无先验情况下无法达到完美的对数级遗憾，但UCB-NOM算法能实现近对数级性能，且在具备先验知识时可达到最优的对数级遗憾，且该遗憾界与状态数无关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在马尔可夫多臂老虎机问题中，当状态不可观测且决策周期受限时，如何最小化遗憾（regret）是一个具有挑战性的问题。传统的后悔基准（纯策略）在复杂环境下难以达到，研究旨在探讨在这种约束下，如何设计有效的学习算法以逼近最优策略，并分析其遗憾增长率。

Method: 1. 引入了“自退化马尔可夫多臂老虎机”（self-degrading Markovian bandits）这一模型概念，证明了纯策略在此模型中具有渐近最优性。
2. 设计了基于乐观原则的算法UCB-NOM，通过优化策略选择来应对不可观测的状态和决策约束。
3. 通过理论分析证明了该算法在不同先验知识假设下的遗憾上界，并证明了其对状态数是不敏感的。

Result: 1. 证明了在无先验知识时，稀疏切换算法的遗憾必然以超对数级（ω(log T)）增长。
2. 提出的UCB-NOM算法在无先验知识情况下实现了近对数级的遗憾。
3. 当拥有关于臂的偏差函数（bias function）的先验知识时，UCB-NOM可实现严格的O(log T)遗憾。
4. 证明了遗憾界与马尔可夫链的状态数量无关，表现出良好的扩展性。

Conclusion: 本文的研究结果表明，对于自退化马尔可夫多臂老虎机问题，状态不可观测性是一个相对较小的问题。即使在无法达到经典对数级遗憾的情况下，通过设计的UCB-NOM算法，依然可以获得近对数级的遗憾界。若结合先验知识，则能实现最优的对数级遗憾。该研究为理解不可观测马尔可夫决策过程中的后悔最小化提供了理论基础。

Abstract: This paper studies the problem of regret minimization in Markovian bandits with \emph{non-observable states} and possibly \emph{constrained} decision epochs. The focus is restricted to a ``pure'' regret benchmark, that compares the performance of the learning algorithm to the best \emph{pure policy} which -- akin to optimal policies of stochastic bandits -- picks the optimal arm from start to finish without ever switching. We introduce a generalization of rested Markovian bandits, \emph{self-degrading Markovian bandits}, for which pure policies are always asymptotically optimal.We show that without prior knowledge on the underlying bandit, the regret of algorithms that switch arms rarely necessarily scales super-logarithmically for every bandit, i.e., as $ω(\log(T))$, where $T$ is the learning horizon. Despite the unreachability of the logarithmic regime, we design UCB-NOM, an optimistic algorithm inspired by UCB, of which the regret is nearly logarithmic. Lastly, we show that given prior knowledge on the Markovian bandit in the form of a bound on the bias functions of its arm, a proper instantiation of UCB-NOM achieves $O(\log(T))$ regret. We further show that this prior knowledge allows for a $O(\sqrt{T \log(T)})$ worst-case regret bound for UCB-NOM. Notably, our regret bounds do not depend on the number of states of the underlying Markov chains. Our findings suggest that the non-observability of states is a mild inconvenience in self-degrading Markovian bandits.

</details>


### [75] [Prism Transformer: Progressive Head Schedules for Hierarchical Attention Processing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27449)
*Shubham Aggarwal*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Prism Transformer打破了传统模型各层头数一致的限制，通过在浅层使用宽头捕捉局部特征、深层使用窄头提取专门特征的渐进式分配策略，在不增加计算和参数负担的情况下，显著提升了模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的Transformer在每一层均分隐藏维度，导致所有头的表示子空间维度固定。作者认为这种均匀分配策略是一种结构性瓶颈，限制了早期层头捕捉复杂、高维上下文模式的能力。

Method: 提出了一种名为“Prism Transformer”的新型架构，其核心在于采用“渐进式头数调度”（progressive head schedule）。该方法不再要求每层具有相同的头数，而是随着深度的增加单调增加头数，从而实现“局部到全局”的表示层次结构：浅层使用少量且维度更宽的头，深层使用大量且维度更窄的头。这一结构调整在保持模型权重矩阵维度和FLOPs预算不变的情况下实现。

Result: 在124M、354M和757M三种不同规模的模型上，Prism Transformer均优于均匀分配的基准模型，在验证集损失上有所降低，并在PIQA、HellaSwag、ARC-Easy和WinoGrande等零样本基准测试中表现更佳。

Conclusion: 研究证明，在保持模型参数量和计算量（FLOPs）不变的前提下，通过采用非均匀的子空间分配策略，可以有效解锁标准Transformer模型中的潜在容量，从而提升模型的整体性能。

Abstract: Multi-head attention conventionally partitions the hidden dimension equally across all heads at every layer, enforcing an identical representational subspace dimension (dh = dmodel/h) throughout the models depth. In this work, we identify this uniform allocation as a fundamental structural bottleneck: due to their restricted dimensional space, early-layer heads are unable to faithfully capture complex, high-dimensional contextual patterns. To resolve this, we introduce the Prism Transformer, a novel architectural paradigm that replaces the static, uniform head configuration with a progressive head schedule. By monotonically increasing the head count across layers, the Prism Transformer naturally establishes a local-to-global representational hierarchy: early layers leverage fewer, exceptionally wide heads to capture complex, local compositional patterns, while deep layers deploy many, narrow heads to decompose these patterns into specialized linguistic features. Crucially, this structural shift is parameter-neutral, compute-neutral, and introduces zero training or inference overhead, preserving identical weight matrices and FLOP budgets as the standard Transformer. Across three model scales (124M, 354M, and 757M), the Prism Transformer consistently outperforms uniform baselines, achieving consistent reductions in validation loss alongside consistent gains on downstream zero-shot benchmarks (including PIQA, HellaSwag, ARC-Easy, and WinoGrande). Our findings demonstrate that non-uniform subspace allocation unlocks latent capacity within the standard Transformer budget, enabling more effective use of model capacity.

</details>


### [76] [Operator Learning for Cubic Nonlinear Schrödinger Equation on Periodic Domains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27459)
*Emmanuel E. Oguadimma,Victory C. Obieke,Xueying Yu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 研究提出了一种针对二维非线性薛定谔方程的几何感知傅里叶神经算子，成功捕捉了不同几何纵横比导致的独特高频动力学级联行为，证明了神经算子在模拟非线性色散偏微分方程频谱传输现象中的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在二维平坦环面上，非线性薛定谔方程（NLS）的解行为高度依赖于环面的纵横比。有理与无理几何结构会导致截然不同的高频级联（cascade）行为，研究旨在利用深度学习方法在数据驱动的层面上探索并准确预测这些受几何影响的动力学特征。

Method: 提出了一种几何条件化的傅里叶神经算子（FNO），将解的实部、虚部及环面纵横比参数（ω²）作为输入。该模型被训练为近似一步解算子，并利用傅里叶伪谱法在随机相位初值数据上进行训练与验证。此外，通过消融实验评估了傅里叶模态、激活函数、层深及几何条件化的具体作用。

Result: 数值实验表明，该模型不仅能准确捕捉不同环面上的核心解动力学，还成功重现了索伯列夫范数（Sobolev norm）的特有行为，即有理环面上更显著的H²增长和无理环面上更受限的行为。实验证实，引入几何参数ω²可显著提高长期预测的准确性。

Conclusion: 本研究证实了基于傅里叶神经算子（FNO）的几何感知学习框架在处理非线性色散偏微分方程（PDE）中的有效性，特别是在捕捉不同几何形状（有理与无理环面）下的复杂频谱传输现象方面表现优异。通过显式引入几何参数，该模型能够成功再现理论预测的索伯列夫范数增长差异，为数据驱动研究PDE动力学提供了有力工具。

Abstract: We consider the cubic nonlinear Schrödinger (NLS) equation on two-dimensional flat tori with varying aspect ratios. In this formulation, the choice of aspect ratio governs the Fourier resonance structure, so rational and irrational geometries can exhibit different high-frequency cascade behaviors. We present a geometry-conditioned Fourier neural operator (FNO) for the cubic defocusing NLS equation, where the input consists of the real and imaginary parts of the solution together with the aspect-ratio parameter \(ω^2\). The model is trained to approximate the one-step solution operator and is evaluated on unseen trajectories generated from random-phase initial data using Fourier pseudospectral method. Our numerical experiments show that the learned operator captures the main solution dynamics on both tori and reproduces the distinct Sobolev norm behavior of the two geometries, with stronger \(H^2\)-growth on the rational torus and more constrained behavior on the irrational torus, consistent with the findings of \cite{hrabski2021energy}. We perform ablation studies to examine the roles of retained Fourier modes, activation functions, Fourier-layer depth, and explicit geometry conditioning. The results indicate that including $ω^2$ improves long-time predictive accuracy, especially for the rational geometry, and supports the use of geometry-aware neural operators for learning spectral-transfer phenomena in nonlinear dispersive partial differential equations.
